                                    C.onPreParse = function(eventName, result) {
                    var positions = result.ps();
                    var pos, posPrefix, posItem, posSettings, nativePosSettings, displayPosSettings, newPosSettings, advTextId, cleanId;
                    var geminiFedPos = ['MAST', 'WFPAD', 'LREC3', 'INBODY'];
                    var adContainerClass = ["caas-da-incremental","darla-container","da-container"];
                    var isGeminiFedPos = false;
                    var isPositionValid = false;
                    var hasAdContainerClass = false;
                    for (i = 0, l = positions.length; i < l; i++) {
                        pos = positions[i];
                        if (!pos) {
                            continue;
                        }
                        posItem = result.item(pos);
                        posSettings = DARLA.posSettings(pos);
                        posPrefix = pos.split('-')[0];
                        isPositionValid =
                            posItem &&
                            !posItem.hasErr &&
                            posItem.size + '' !== '1x1' &&
                            posItem.meta &&
                            posItem.meta.y &&
                            posItem.meta.y.size &&
                            posItem.meta.y.size + '' !== '1x1';
                        if (typeof geminiFedPos.some !== 'undefined' && typeof geminiFedPos.some === 'function') {
                            isGeminiFedPos = geminiFedPos.some(function(fedPos) {
                                return pos.indexOf(fedPos) === 0;
                            });
                        }
                        if (isPositionValid && isGeminiFedPos) {
                            advTextId = document.getElementById('sdaAdvText-' + pos);
                            nativePosSettings = DARLA.posSettings(posPrefix + '-NATIVE-PH');
                            displayPosSettings = DARLA.posSettings(posPrefix + '-DISPLAY-PH');
                            if (posItem && posItem.serveType == 10 && nativePosSettings && nativePosSettings.dest) {
                                newPosSettings = nativePosSettings;
                                if (advTextId) { 
                                    advTextId.style.display = 'none';
                                }
                            } else if (displayPosSettings && displayPosSettings.dest) {
                                newPosSettings = displayPosSettings;
                                if (advTextId) { 
                                    advTextId.style.display = 'block';
                                }
                            }
                            if (newPosSettings && posSettings) {
                                newPosSettings.id = pos;
                                newPosSettings.pos = pos;
                                newPosSettings.clean = posSettings.clean;
                                newPosSettings.dest = posSettings.dest;
                                cleanId = document.getElementById(newPosSettings.clean);

                                if (cleanId && cleanId.parentNode && cleanId.parentNode.classList) {
                                    cleanId.parentNode.classList.add('da-parsed', posPrefix);
                                }

                                DARLA.addPos(newPosSettings);
                            }
                        }
                        // Ad position fails then add error class for styling
                        if (!isPositionValid) {
                            cleanId = document.getElementById(posSettings.clean);

                            if (cleanId &&
                                cleanId.parentNode &&
                                cleanId.parentNode.classList &&
                                typeof adContainerClass.some === 'function' ) {

                                hasAdContainerClass = adContainerClass.some(function(parentClass) {
                                    return cleanId.parentNode.classList.contains(parentClass);
                                });
                                hasAdContainerClass && cleanId.parentNode.classList.add('da-error', posPrefix);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };

            var isWhitelistedNonUBAPos = false;
            if (typeof whitelistedNonUBAPositions.some !== 'undefined' && typeof whitelistedNonUBAPositions.some === 'function') {
                isWhitelistedNonUBAPos = whitelistedNonUBAPositions.some(function(wPos) {
                    return position.indexOf(wPos) === 0;
                });
            }
            var isNonUBAadBlockPos = false && isWhitelistedNonUBAPos;
            var isGeminiFedPos = false;
            var posPrefix = position.split('-')[0];
            if (typeof geminiFedPos.some !== 'undefined' && typeof geminiFedPos.some === 'function') {
                isGeminiFedPos = geminiFedPos.some(function(fedPos) {
                    return position.indexOf(fedPos) === 0;
                });
            }

            if (isSlugEnablePos || isNonUBAadBlockPos || position.indexOf('INARTICLE') >= 0 || position.indexOf('UBA') >= 0) {
                var isUBA = position.indexOf('UBA') >= 0;
                if (isPositionValid) {
                    if (inaDiv && !nodeIdDiv) {
                        var inaText = document.createElement('div');
                        var advTextInnerHTML = '';
                        inaText.id = nodeId;
                        inaText.style.fontSize = isUBA || isNonUBAadBlockPos ? '13px' : '10px';
                        inaText.style.textAlign = isUBA || isNonUBAadBlockPos ? 'left' : 'center';
                        if (isUBA) {
                            var ubaClean = inaDiv.parentElement;
                            inaText.style.margin = 'auto';
                            if (posSetting.w) {
                                inaText.style.width = posSetting.w + 'px';
                            }
                            if (ubaClean && ubaClean.classList && ubaClean.classList.contains && !ubaClean.classList.contains('uba-container')) {
                                ubaClean.classList.add('uba-container');
                            }
                        }
                        if (isUBA || isNonUBAadBlockPos) {
                            advTextInnerHTML = advText;
                        } else if (isSlugEnablePos) {
                            advTextInnerHTML = advText.toUpperCase();
                        } else {
                            advTextInnerHTML = '- ' + advText.toUpperCase() + ' -';
                        }
                        inaText.innerHTML = advTextInnerHTML;
                        inaDiv.parentElement.insertBefore(inaText, inaDiv);
                    } else if (nodeIdDiv) { // as INARTICLE would fall here we need show adv text
                        nodeIdDiv.style.display = 'block';
                    }
                }
            }

            if (isPositionValid) {
                if (isGeminiFedPos && cleanId && cleanId.parentNode && cleanId.parentNode.classList) {
                    cleanId.parentNode.classList.add(position);
                }
                if (nodeIdDiv && posItem && posItem.serveType != 10) {

                    return;
                }

                var firstBatchPos = [];

                // goes through the positions in the firstRender array and removes any duplicates from the prefetched positions
                for (var i = 0; i < firstRender.length; i++) {
                    var position = firstRender[i];
                    var index = prefetchedPos.indexOf(position);
                    if (index >= 0) {
                        firstBatchPos = firstBatchPos.concat(prefetchedPos.splice(index, 1));
                    }
                };

                if (firstBatchPos.length > 0) {
                    var renderWithRetry = function(pos) {
                        if (DARLA.inProgress()) {
                            var waittime = 600, maxwait = 100, deferRetry = 0, interval;
                            interval = setInterval(function() {
                                deferRetry ++;
                                if (!DARLA.inProgress()) {
                                    clearInterval(interval);
                                    // Render the remaining ads
                                    DARLA.render(pos);
                                }
                                if (deferRetry > maxwait) {
                                    DARLA.abort();
                                    clearInterval(interval);
                                    DARLA.render(pos);
                                }
                            }, waittime);
                        } else {
                            // Render the remaining ads
                            DARLA.render(pos);
                        }
                    }

                    // it will render the positions that were in the firstRender array
                    renderWithRetry(firstBatchPos);
                    // after an interval render the remaining prefetched positions
                    setTimeout(renderWithRetry, 3000, prefetchedPos);
                } else {
                    // non of the firstBatchPos in prefetchedPos then render whatever we have
                    DARLA.render();
                }
            } else {
                // if firstRender is empty, it will render all the ads
                DARLA.render();
            }

                    var visibilityChange = 'visibilitychange';

                    var UNDEFINED = 'undefined';
                    if (typeof document.mozHidden !== UNDEFINED) {
                        hidden = 'mozHidden';
                        visibilityChange = 'moz' + visibilityChange;
                    } else if (typeof document.msHidden !== UNDEFINED) {
                        hidden = 'msHidden';
                        visibilityChange = 'ms' + visibilityChange;
                    } else if (typeof document.webkitHidden !== UNDEFINED) {
                        hidden = 'webkitHidden';
                        visibilityChange = 'webkit' + visibilityChange;
                    }
                    return {
                        hidden: hidden,
                        visibilityChange: visibilityChange
                    };
                })();

                var dispatchWindowEvent = function (eventName) {
                    var event;

                    if (typeof dispatchEvent === 'undefined') {
                        return;
                    }

                    if (typeof(Event) === 'function') {
                        event = new Event(eventName);
                    } else {
                        event = document.createEvent('Event');
                        event.initEvent(eventName, true, true);

                    dispatchEvent(event);

                var handleFocus = function () {

                        if (isViewerOpen) {

                            if (!viewerEventSettings || !viewerEventSettings.ps) {

                                                    }

                                                    if (adCallPositions.indexOf(nAdPos) < 0) {

                                                    }
                                                });
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            [].concat(adBoostGroupConf[adPos].extrapositions).forEach(function (nAdPos) {
                                                if (adCallPositions.indexOf(nAdPos) < 0) {

                var darlaOnreadyPoll = function darlaOnreadyPoll() {
                    var timeout = Number(new Date()) + 20000;
                    var interval = 300;

                    (function condition() {
                        if (window.DARLA) {
                            darlaOnready();
                        } else if (Number(new Date()) < timeout) {
                            setTimeout(condition, interval);
                        } else {
                            // NoAds

/**

var removeSlot = function (slot, googletag, slotsState) {

            delete slotsState.viewer[REFRESHABLE_SLOT_GROUP][id];
        }
    });
};
/**
 * Adds timer to ad slot config if there is none
 * @param {PositionsConfigPair} positions
 * @param {number} rotationTimer
 * @return {PositionsConfigPair}
 */
function addDefaultTimerToDefinitions(positions, rotationTimer) {
    var results = {};
    for (var id in positions) {
        if (positions.hasOwnProperty(id)) {
            results[id] = cloneDeep(positions[id]);
            if (results[id].targeting && results[id].targeting.length) {
                addDefaultFetchKVs(results[id]);
                continue;
            }
            results[id].targeting = [
                { key: REFRESH_TIMER, value: rotationTimer },
            ];
            addDefaultFetchKVs(results[id]);
        }
    }
    return results;
}
/**
 * Adds fetch KVs to ad slot config if there is none

 * @return {AdConfig<string>}

function addDefaultFetchKVs(position) {

}

            var slotConfig = getSingleSlotConfig(slotId, slotAdUnitPath, slotRenderedSize_1, window);
            // execute
            (_b = (_a = window === null || window === void 0 ? void 0 : window.gpt) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.util) === null || _b === void 0 ? void 0 : _b.execute(slotConfig);
        }
    });
}
function getSingleSlotConfig(id, path, size, window) {
    var _a;
    var position = (_a = {},
        _a[id] = { id: id, path: path, size: size },
        _a);
    var rotationTimer = window.gpt.GPTconfig.rotationTimer || DEFAULT_ROTATION_TIMER;
    var slotConfig = {
        overrideFuncs: {
            collapseEmptyDivs: {
                arguments: [],
                enabled: true,
                name: "collapseEmptyDivs"
            }
        },
        positions: addDefaultTimerToDefinitions(position, rotationTimer),
        refreshable: true,
        lmsid: getLmsidValue(window)
    };
    return slotConfig;
}
/**
* Multiple slots may get defined one after the another
* Leading to multiple refresh invocations
* Thus we are batch slots
* @param {Slot[]} slots array
* @param {AdSlotsGroup} slotQueueMap array
*/
function enqueueRefreshableSlots(slots, slotsQueueMap) {
    // always push slots into the queue
    slots.forEach(function (slot) {
        // to avoid duplicate slots, adding each slot the queue map
        slotsQueueMap[slot.getSlotElementId()] = slot;
    });
}
/**
* 1. Pick all slots from the queue inview
* 2. call refresh for the slots
* @param {Window} WIN
* @param {Function} refresh
*/
function callRefreshAndClearQ(WIN, refreshFunc) {
    var googletag = WIN.googletag, gpt = WIN.gpt;
    var slotsQueueMap = gpt.slotsQueueMap, adSlots = gpt.adSlots;
    // get all the slots from queue that are in view
    var slots = Object.values(slotsQueueMap).filter(function (item) {
        var slotId = item.getSlotElementId();
        if (isVisibleInViewport(slotId, WIN)) {
            delete slotsQueueMap[slotId];
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    });
    slots.length && refreshFunc(slots, googletag, adSlots);
}

function enableAdCollapse() {
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag
            .pubads()
            .addEventListener(GPT_EVENTS.slotRenderEnded, function (event) {
            var slot = event.slot;
            if (event.isEmpty) {
                collapseSlotContainer(document, slot);
                // remove slot so that it cannot be rotated
                removeSlot(slot, googletag, adSlots);
            }
        });
    });
}
function refreshInView() {
    var inViewItems = [];
    var indexRefreshableSlots = getSlotsFromSlotsGroup(INDEX_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP);
    var viewerRefreshableSlots = getSlotsFromSlotsGroup(VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP);
    var slotsEligibleForRefresh = [].concat(indexRefreshableSlots, viewerRefreshableSlots);
    // collect in-viewport slots that eligible for refresh
    slotsEligibleForRefresh.forEach(function (slot) {
        var slotId = slot.getSlotElementId();
        if (isVisibleInViewport(slotId, WIN)) {
            inViewItems.push(slot);
        }
    });
    var slots = adRefreshKeyValuesToSlots(inViewItems, REFRESH_TYPES.tabSwitch);
    // TODO: remove if condition after feature GA
    if (enableGPTRefreshQ) {
        enqueueRefreshableSlots(slots, gpt.slotsQueueMap);
        callRefreshAndClearQ(WIN, refresh);
    }
    else {
        refresh(slots, WIN.googletag, adSlots);
    }
}
function initViewablePositionListener() {
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag
            .pubads()
            .addEventListener(GPT_EVENTS.slotVisibilityChanged, function (event) {
            var slot = event.slot;
            var eligibleForRefresh = slot.getTargeting(ELIGIBLE_FOR_REQUEST)[0];
            // only autorefresh slots that have autorefresh targeting
            var slotTimer = slot.getTargeting(REFRESH_TIMER);
            // if slot eligible for refresh and has more than 0% viewability
            if (slotTimer.length &&
                event.inViewPercentage &&
                (eligibleForRefresh || isTimeToRefresh(slot))) {
                var refreshType = enableGPTRefreshQ
                    ? REFRESH_TYPES.userEvent
                    : REFRESH_TYPES.time;
                var slots = adRefreshKeyValuesToSlots([slot], refreshType);
                if (enableGPTRefreshQ) {
                    enqueueRefreshableSlots(slots, gpt.slotsQueueMap); // function to batch the slots
                }
                else {
                    refresh(slots, WIN.googletag, adSlots);
                }
            }
        });
    });
}
function setAutoRotation() {
    // Number of seconds to wait after the slot becomes viewable.
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag
            .pubads()
            .addEventListener(GPT_EVENTS.impressionViewable, function (event) {
            var slot = event.slot;
            // only ads with a refresh key are eligible for auto rotation
            var slotTimer = slot.getTargeting(REFRESH_TIMER);
            if (slotTimer.length) {
                slot.setTargeting(SLOT_VIEWED, 'true');
                slot.setTargeting(LAST_REQUESTED, Date.now());
                var timeToWait = slotTimer[0];
                setTimeout(function () {
                    rotatePosition(slot);
                }, timeToWait * 1000);
            }
        });
    });
}
function rotatePosition(slot) {
    var id = slot.getSlotElementId();
    var elem = document.getElementById(id);
    // check if slot still on the page
    if (elem) {
        var timeToRefresh = isTimeToRefresh(slot);
        if (enableGPTRefreshQ && timeToRefresh) {
            var slots = adRefreshKeyValuesToSlots([slot], REFRESH_TYPES.userEvent);
            enqueueRefreshableSlots(slots, gpt.slotsQueueMap);
            return;
        }
        // TODO: remove the following code if batch works with no issues
        // check if slot inview
        var inView = isVisibleInViewport(id, WIN);
        if (inView && timeToRefresh) {
            var slots = adRefreshKeyValuesToSlots([slot]);
            refresh(slots, WIN.googletag, adSlots);
        }
        else {
            // mark ad as eligible for being refreshed if isTimeToRefresh
            // but not inview so it will be picked up by initViewablePositionListener
            slot.setTargeting(ELIGIBLE_FOR_REQUEST, timeToRefresh);
        }
    }
}
function isTimeToRefresh(slot) {
    var slotTimer = slot.getTargeting(REFRESH_TIMER);
    if (slotTimer.length) {
        var timeToWait = slotTimer[0];
        var lastRequested = slot.getTargeting(LAST_REQUESTED)[0];
        // check how long ago ad was last requested.
        var refreshDiff = (Date.now() - lastRequested) / 1000;
        // has it been long enough to refresh?
        return timeToWait <= refreshDiff;
    }
    return false;
}
function refreshModalSlots() {
    // refresh viewer slots when viewer content changes
    if (gpt.viewerOpened) {
        var slots = adRefreshKeyValuesToSlots(getSlotsFromSlotsGroup(VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP), REFRESH_TYPES.viewerContentChanged, false);
        if (enableGPTRefreshQ) {
            enqueueRefreshableSlots(slots, gpt.slotsQueueMap);
        }
        else {
            refresh(slots, WIN.googletag, adSlots);
        }
    }
}
function initSlotRequestTimers() {
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag
            .pubads()
            .addEventListener(GPT_EVENTS.slotRequested, function (event) {
            var slot = event.slot;
            var isViewed = slot.getTargeting(SLOT_VIEWED)[0];
            if (isViewed) {
                slot.setTargeting(LAST_REQUESTED, Date.now());
                slot.setTargeting(ELIGIBLE_FOR_REQUEST, false);
            }
        });
    });
}
/**
 * Loads ad slots on various events
 * @param {Object} data from event
 */
function onEventGPTHandler(data) {
    var _a;
    var type = data.type;
    var dataElem = data.elem;
    var elem = type === EVENTS.caasSidekick
        ? dataElem.parentNode
        : ((_a = data.meta.targetElem) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.parentNode) || dataElem.parentNode;
    if (!elem || (type === EVENTS.caasArticle && !isSiteGPTenabled(data))) {
        return;
    }
    var adDefinitions;
    if (type === EVENTS.darlaComplete) {
        adDefinitions = getGPTAdDefinitionsFromConfig(data);
    }
    else {
        adDefinitions = getGPTAdDefinitionsFromElem(elem, GPT_NATIVE_AD_IDENTIFIER);
    }
    var refreshable = false;
    if (type === EVENTS.darlaComplete || type === EVENTS.caasArticle) {
        // refresh the yield ads from DARLA (LDRB3) and from article content (INBODYLRECs)
        refreshable = true;
    }
    var eventsGPTconfig = {
        lmsid: getLmsidValue(WIN),
        overrideFuncs: {
            collapseEmptyDivs: {
                arguments: [],
                enabled: false,
                name: 'collapseEmptyDivs',
            },
        },
        positions: {},
        refreshable: refreshable,
    };
    adDefinitions.forEach(function (_a) {
        var id = _a.id, path = _a.path, size = _a.size; _a.lazyload; var _b = _a.targeting, targeting = _b === void 0 ? [] : _b;
        if (type === EVENTS.caasSidekick) {
            // always re-render yield ads for sidekick placement
            var sidekickSlot_1 = NATIVE_SLOTS_GROUP[id];
            googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                googletag.destroySlots([sidekickSlot_1]);
                delete NATIVE_SLOTS_GROUP[id];
            });
        }
        eventsGPTconfig.positions[id] = {
            id: id,
            path: path,
            size: size,
            targeting: targeting,
        };
    });
    var lazyloadAds = adDefinitions.some(function (dd) {
        return dd.lazyload;
    });
    if (lazyloadAds) {
        eventsGPTconfig.overrideFuncs.enableLazyLoad = {
            arguments: [
                {
                    fetchMarginPercent: 50,
                    mobileScaling: 2.0,
                    renderMarginPercent: 50,
                },
            ],
            enabled: true,
            name: 'enableLazyLoad',
        };
    }
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        try {
            execute(eventsGPTconfig);
        }
        catch (e) {
            beacon(BeaconType.ERROR, {
                eventName: 'Yieldtest',
                eventType: 'onEventGPTHandler-error',
                lang: 'en-US',
                message: JSON.stringify(e),
                region: 'US',
                rid: WIN.YAHOO.context.rid,
            });
        }
    });
}

            });

    });

        }
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            var _a, _b;
            try {
                execute(slotsConfig_1);
            }
            catch (e) {
                beacon(BeaconType.ERROR, {
                    eventName: 'Yieldtest',
                    eventType: 'loadIndexDisplaySlots-error',
                    lang: 'en-US',
                    message: JSON.stringify(e),
                    region: 'US',
                    rid: (_b = (_a = WIN.YAHOO) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.context) === null || _b === void 0 ? void 0 : _b.rid,

}
/**
 * Cleans up after modal/viewer close
 */
function handleViewerClose() {
    gpt.viewerOpened = false;
    setTargetAfterModalTransition(WIN, googletag);
    if (WIN.DARLA) {
        var hpViewerEvtSettings = WIN.DARLA.evtSettings('homepage-viewer');
        if (hpViewerEvtSettings && hpViewerEvtSettings.ps) {
            WIN.DARLA.del('homepage-viewer');
        }
    }
    updatedHBVariables();
    // destroy all viewerslots when viewer closed
    var slotsToDestroy = getSlotsFromSlotsGroup(VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP);
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag.destroySlots(slotsToDestroy);
        Object.keys(VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP).forEach(function (key) { return delete VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP[key]; });
    });
    // refresh index page positions if any on viewer close
    if (Object.keys(INDEX_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP).length) {
        var slots = adRefreshKeyValuesToSlots(getSlotsFromSlotsGroup(INDEX_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP), REFRESH_TYPES.viewerClosed, false);
        refresh(slots, WIN.googletag, adSlots);
    }
}

/**
 * Extract gpt data from wafer-darla event
 * @param {object} config config taken from wafer event
 * @returns {AdConfig<string>[]} array of slot definitions
 */
function getGPTAdDefinitionsFromConfig(data) {
    var _a;
    var darlaConfig = data && data.meta && data.meta.darlaConfig;
    if (darlaConfig) {
        var yieldAdSlot = (_a = darlaConfig.yieldAd) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.slot;
        var id = getYieldId(yieldAdSlot.id);
        var res = [
            {
                id: id,
                lazyload: true,
                path: yieldAdSlot.path,
                size: yieldAdSlot.size,
                targeting: yieldAdSlot.targeting || [
                    { key: REFRESH_TIMER, value: ROTATION_TIMER },
                ],
            },
        ];
        data.elem.id = id;
        return res;
    }
    return [];
}
/**
 * Parse gpt ad placeholders from a DOM node and return a list of gpt ad definition objects
 * @param {HTMLElement} node element loaded in from wafer event
 * @param {string} identifier ad slot container class name
 * @returns {AdConfig[]} array of slot definitions
 */
function getGPTAdDefinitionsFromElem(node, identifier) {
    var classSelector = ".".concat(identifier);
    var adPlaceholders = node.querySelectorAll(classSelector);
    if (!adPlaceholders) {
        return;
    }
    return Array.from(adPlaceholders).map(function (adPlaceholder) {
        var _a = adPlaceholder.dataset, adUnitPath = _a.adUnitPath, adUnitSize = _a.adUnitSize, adUnitLazyload = _a.adUnitLazyload, adUnitTargeting = _a.adUnitTargeting;
        var id = adPlaceholder.id;
        var adUnitSizeArr;
        try {
            adUnitSizeArr = JSON.parse(adUnitSize);
        }
        catch (e) {
            beacon(BeaconType.ERROR, {
                eventName: 'Yieldtest',
                eventType: 'getGPTAdDefinitionsFromElem-error',
                lang: 'en-US',
                message: JSON.stringify(e),
                region: 'US',
                rid: WIN.YAHOO.context.rid,
            });
        }
        var adConfig = {
            id: id,
            lazyload: !!adUnitLazyload,
            path: adUnitPath,
            size: adUnitSizeArr,
        };
        if (adUnitTargeting) {
            // @ts-ignore
            adConfig.targeting = adUnitTargeting;
        }
        return adConfig;
    });
}
function updatedHBVariables(adMeta) {
    if (GPTconfig.enableGPTHB) {
        WIN.advBidxc = WIN.advBidxc || {};
        WIN.advBidxc.execute = WIN.advBidxc.execute || [];
        WIN.advBidxc.execute.push(function () {
            var _a, _b;
            WIN.advBidxc.update({
                // Update Yahoo's section name
                mchnm: getLmsidValue(WIN, adMeta),
                spaceid: "".concat((_b = (_a = WIN.YAHOO) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.i13n) === null || _b === void 0 ? void 0 : _b.SPACEID),
                ysec: gpt.viewerOpened ? 'modal' : 'general', // send us the space id
            });
        });
    }
}
function trackPerformance() {
    if (!perfMarker.trackerStatus) {
        perfMarker.trackerStatus = true;
        trackInitMetrics({
            isGAMMNET: !!GPTconfig.enableGPTHB,
            spaceid: getSpaceId(WIN),
        });
    }
    if (GPTconfig.waitOnLoad || perfMarker.fetchStart.status) {
        return;
    }
    // PERF: measure render end
    var onSlotOnload = function (event) {
        if (!perfMarker.slots.length) {
            // we have tracked all OR there is none to track
            googletag
                .pubads()
                .removeEventListener(GPT_EVENTS.slotOnload, onSlotOnload);
        }
        var slotElementId = event.slot.getSlotElementId();
        perfMarker.slots.forEach(function (slot, index) {
            if (slot.id === slotElementId) {
                var renderEnd = WIN.performance.now();
                WIN._adLT.push([slot.marker, Math.round(renderEnd)]);
                perfMarker.slots.splice(index, 1);
            }
        });
    };
    // PERF: measure fetch start
    perfMarker.fetchStart.status = true;
    if (WIN.performance && WIN.performance.now) {
        var fetchStart = WIN.performance.now();
        WIN._adLT.push([perfMarker.fetchStart.marker, Math.round(fetchStart)]);
        googletag
            .pubads()
            .addEventListener(GPT_EVENTS.slotOnload, onSlotOnload);
    }
}
/**
 * Checks if site is enabled for GPT
 * @param {Object} event data
 * @returns {boolean} whether or not the site is eanbled for GPT
 */
function isSiteGPTenabled(event) {
    var _a, _b, _c;
    var adMeta = event ? (_a = event.meta.data) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.adMeta : {};
    var articleSite = (adMeta && adMeta.site) || ((_c = (_b = WIN.YAHOO) === null || _b === void 0 ? void 0 : _b.context) === null || _c === void 0 ? void 0 : _c.site);
    var isAllowed = false;
    if ((typeof GPTconfig.site === 'string' &&
        articleSite === GPTconfig.site) ||
        (Array.isArray(GPTconfig.site) &&
            GPTconfig.site.indexOf(articleSite) !== -1)) {
        isAllowed = true;
    }
    return isAllowed;
}
/**
 * Dispatches requests to GPT for ads based on config
 * @param {Object} config object containing positions, overrideFuncs and boolean for true or false
 */
function execute(config) {
    if (!config.positions || Object.keys(config.positions).length === 0) {
        return;
    }
    var positions = config.positions;
    var overrideFuncs = config.overrideFuncs;
    var refreshable = config.refreshable;
    var newPositionIds = [];
    for (var id in positions) {
        if (positions.hasOwnProperty(id)) {
            if (!NATIVE_SLOTS_GROUP[id] &&
                !INDEX_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP[id] &&
                !VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP[id] &&
                !!document.getElementById(id)) {
                newPositionIds.push(id);
            }
        }
    }
    if (newPositionIds.length === 0) {
        // all positions in gpt config are existed
        return;
    }
    var slotsGroup;
    var INBODYLREC_IDENTIFIER = 'sda-INBODYLREC';
    var isInBodyLrecs = newPositionIds.some(function (newPositionId) {
        return newPositionId.includes(INBODYLREC_IDENTIFIER);
    });
    if (refreshable === false) {
        slotsGroup = NATIVE_SLOTS_GROUP;
    }
    else if (isInBodyLrecs) {
        slotsGroup = gpt.viewerOpened
            ? VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP
            : INDEX_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP;
    }
    else {
        var isViewerPosition = isViewerAd(newPositionIds);
        slotsGroup = isViewerPosition
            ? VIEWER_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP
            : INDEX_DISPLAY_SLOTS_GROUP;
    }
    var newAdSlots = [];
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        // update header bidding variables
        var spaceId = getSpaceId(WIN);
        newPositionIds.forEach(function (newId) {
            var _a = positions[newId], path = _a.path, size = _a.size, id = _a.id, targeting = _a.targeting;
            var newAdSlot = googletag
                .defineSlot(path, size, id)
                .addService(googletag.pubads())
                .setTargeting('position-spaceid', "".concat(spaceId));
            // set any additional slot targeting
            if (targeting && targeting.length) {
                targeting.forEach(function (item) {
                    newAdSlot.setTargeting(item.key, item.value);
                });
            }
            slotsGroup[id] = newAdSlot;
            newAdSlots.push(newAdSlot);
        });
        for (var property in overrideFuncs) {
            if (overrideFuncs.hasOwnProperty(property)) {
                var ovr = overrideFuncs[property];
                if (ovr.enabled) {
                    googletag.pubads()[ovr.name].apply(null, ovr.arguments);
                }
            }
        }
        if (config.lmsid) {
            googletag
                .pubads()
                .setTargeting(LMSID_STR_VALUE.toUpperCase(), config.lmsid);
        }
        // set Page level telemetry
        setPageTarget(WIN, googletag, GPTconfig);
        setTargetAfterModalTransition(WIN, googletag);
        !enableGPTLoadByDisplay && googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
        if (GPTconfig.gamPPID) {
            googletag.pubads().setPublisherProvidedId(GPTconfig.gamPPID);
        }
    });
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        if (newAdSlots.length) {
            trackPerformance();
            googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
            googletag.enableServices();
            enableGPTLoadByDisplay
                ? googletag.display(newAdSlots[0])
                : googletag.pubads().refresh(newAdSlots);
        }
    });
}
// TODO Remove after GM-10845 is resolved
function divNotFoundTelemetry(dfpAdUnitPath, divId) {
    if (enableDivNotFoundLog) {
        beacon(BeaconType.ERROR, {
            eventName: 'Yieldtest',
            eventType: 'divNotFound',
            lang: 'en-US',
            message: JSON.stringify({
                adUnitPath: dfpAdUnitPath,
                divID: divId,
                pageType: gpt.viewerOpened ? 'modal' : 'non-modal',
            }),
            region: 'US',
            rid: WIN.YAHOO.context.rid,
        });
    }
}
function onSlotResponseReceivedOperations() {
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag
            .pubads()
            .addEventListener(GPT_EVENTS.slotResponseReceived, function (event) {
            var slot = event.slot;
            var divId = slot.getSlotElementId();
            var dfpAdUnitPath = slot.getAdUnitPath();
            var divElem = document.getElementById(divId);
            var divPresent = !!divElem;
            if (divPresent) {
                var parentDiv = divElem.parentElement;
                if (parentDiv.classList) {
                    parentDiv.classList.remove('Ht-pl-LDRB', 'Ht-pl-LREC');
                }
            }
            else {
                divNotFoundTelemetry(dfpAdUnitPath, divId);
            }
        });
    });
}
function executeHeaderBidder() {
    // Initialize setup variables
    WIN.advBidxc = WIN.advBidxc || {};
    WIN.advBidxc.timeout = 1e3;
    WIN.advBidxc.customerId = '8CU8A3966';
    WIN.advBidxc.domain = WIN.location.hostname;
    WIN.advBidxc.version = 7.1;
    WIN.advBidxc.startTime = new Date().getTime();
    WIN.advBidxc.mchnm = getLmsidValue(WIN); // Custom-channel reporting
    WIN.advBidxc.ysec = gpt.viewerOpened ? 'modal' : 'general'; // Set Y! section name
    WIN.advBidxc.spaceid = getSpaceId(WIN); // Set Y! section name
    function loadScript(tagSrc, id) {
        var scriptTag = document.createElement('script');
        var placeTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
        scriptTag.type = 'text/javascript';
        scriptTag.async = true;
        scriptTag.src = tagSrc;
        scriptTag.id = id;
        placeTag.parentNode.insertBefore(scriptTag, placeTag);
    }
    // loads Google's GAM API (gpt.js) for finalizing auction on GAM
    function loadGPT() {
        if (!WIN.advBidxc.isAdServerLoaded) {
            loadScript('https://securepubads.g.doubleclick.net/tag/js/gpt.js', 'gpt-script');
            WIN.advBidxc.isAdServerLoaded = true;
        }
    }
    // Set timeout for loading GAM's API gpt.js
    WIN.advBidxc.loadGPT = setTimeout(loadGPT, WIN.advBidxc.timeout); // Load the HB wrapper JS
    var abSrc = 'https://hbx.media.net/bidexchange.js?cid=' +
        WIN.advBidxc.customerId +
        '&version=' +
        WIN.advBidxc.version +
        '&dn=' +
        WIN.advBidxc.domain +
        '&ysec=' +
        WIN.advBidxc.ysec;
    loadScript(abSrc, 'mnet-script');
}
function forceSafeFrame() {
    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
        googletag.pubads().setForceSafeFrame(true);
        googletag.pubads().setSafeFrameConfig({
            allowOverlayExpansion: false,
            allowPushExpansion: false,
            sandbox: true,
        });
    });
}

                    var preProcess = function() {
                        // Override the ad load time as the ad module's load time
                        var darlaAdTimings = [];
                        var adTiming;
                        var aft2StartRender = w.YAFT.AFT2.getAFT2StartRender() - 800;
                        if (typeof w._adLT !== 'undefined') {
                            for (var i = 0; i < w._adLT.length; i++) {
                                adTiming = w._adLT[i];
                                var adIdAction = adTiming[0];
                                var adTime = adTiming[1];
                                var adAction = adIdAction.indexOf('ADSTART_') > -1 ? 'start' : 'end';
                                var adId = '';

                                if (adAction === 'start') {
                                    adId = adIdAction.replace('ADSTART_', '');
                                    darlaAdTimings[adId] = {
                                        started: adTime,
                                        loaded: 0
                                    };
                                } else {
                                    adId = adIdAction.replace('ADEND_', '');
                                    if (typeof darlaAdTimings[adId] !== 'undefined') {
                                        darlaAdTimings[adId].loaded = adTime;
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            for (var adObj in darlaAdTimings) {
                                if (darlaAdTimings.hasOwnProperty(adObj) && whiteListedAds && typeof whiteListedAds[adObj] !== undefined) {
                                    var adStartTime = darlaAdTimings[adObj].started;
                                    var adLoadTime = darlaAdTimings[adObj].loaded || w.performance.now();
                                    if (aft2StartRender > adStartTime) {continue;}
                                    w.YAFT.triggerCustomTiming(whiteListedAds[adObj], adStartTime, adLoadTime);
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        // Override the video load time as the module's load time
                        if (typeof w._videoLT !== 'undefined') {
                            for (var key in w._videoLT) {
                                if (w._videoLT.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                                    w.YAFT.triggerCustomTiming(key, w._videoLT[key].startTime, w._videoLT[key].loadTime || w.performance.now());
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    };

                    var setPagePerfDataForTrackModules = function(pagePerfData) {
                        var trackModulesPerfMark = w.performance.getEntriesByType('mark');
                        if (trackModulesPerfMark) {
                            var trackModules = yaftConfig.trackModulesMap;
                            if (trackModules) {
                                var trackModuleNames = [];
                                for (var trackModule in trackModules) {
                                    if (trackModules.hasOwnProperty(trackModule)) {
                                        trackModuleNames.push(trackModule);
                                    }
                                }
                                if (trackModuleNames.length > 0) {
                                    for (var t = 0; t < trackModulesPerfMark.length; t++) {
                                        var moduleMark = trackModulesPerfMark[t];
                                        if (trackModuleNames.indexOf(moduleMark.name) !== -1) {
                                            pagePerfData[trackModules[moduleMark.name]] = Math.round(moduleMark.startTime);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    yaftConfig.preProcess = preProcess;
                    w.YAFT.init(yaftConfig, function(data, error) {
                        if (!error && w.rapidInstance) {
                            var aft = Math.round(data.aft);
                            var initialPageLoad = {
                                AFT: aft,
                                AFT1: aft,
                                AFTNOAD: Math.round(data.aftNoAd),
                                STR: Math.round(data.startRender),
                                VIC: data.visuallyComplete,
                                PLT: data.pageLoadTime,
                                DOMC: data.domElementsCount,
                                HTTPC: data.httpRequests.count,
                                CP: Math.round(data.totalCoveragePercentage),
                                NCP: Math.round(data.normTotalCoveragePercentage)
                            };
                            var customPerfData = {};
                            var pagePerfData = {};
                            if ( window._adLT) {
                                for (var i = 0; i < _adLT.length; i++) {
                                    pagePerfData[_adLT[i][0]]  = _adLT[i][1];
                                }
                            }
                            setPagePerfDataForTrackModules(pagePerfData);
                            // Track user connection type
                            var navConnection = navigator && (navigator.connection || navigator.mozConnection || navigator.webkitConnection) || {};
                            pagePerfData['CONNECTION_TYPE'] = navConnection.effectiveType || 'unknown';
                                                        
                            customPerfData['utm'] = pagePerfData;
                            var perfData = {
                                perf_commontime: {
                                    initialPageLoad: initialPageLoad
                                },
                                perf_usertime: customPerfData
                            };

                            w.rapidInstance.beaconPerformanceData(perfData);
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
        }
    })(window);

var ubDetection = function() {
    // primary check: create node has sensitive id on the fly
    const decoyId = 'my-ads';
    const decoyNode = document.createElement('div');
    decoyNode.setAttribute('id', decoyId);
    decoyNode.innerHTML = decoyId;
    document.body.appendChild(decoyNode);
    
    const decoyNodeIns = document.querySelector(`#${decoyId}`);
    if (decoyNodeIns && decoyNodeIns.offsetHeight === 0) {
        decoyNodeIns.remove();
        return true;
    }
    decoyNodeIns.remove();
    
    // additional check: check all necessary ad pos dimension
    if (shouldCheckPosition) {
        const { positions } = dabConfig;
        let adposNodeCount = 0;
        let hidenPosNodeCount = 0;
        
        for (const position of positions) {
            const adposNode = document.querySelector(`#${position}`);
            if (adposNode) {
                adposNodeCount += 1;
                if (adposNode.offsetHeight === 0) {
                    hidenPosNodeCount += 1;
                }
            }
        }

        if (adposNodeCount > 0 && adposNodeCount === hidenPosNodeCount) {
            return true;
        }
    }
    return false;
}

var initABDetection = function() {
    var daTrk = '0';
    var cExpiry = 0;
    var expires = new Date();

    /* General AB Check */
    var abSelector = document.getElementById('advertisement-thamba');
    if (!abSelector) {
        daTrk = '1';
        cExpiry = cookieDuration;
    }

    /* Specific AB Check */
    if (dabConfig.enableUBDetection) {
        const isUBActive = ubDetection();
        if (isUBActive) {
            daTrk = '1';
            cExpiry = cookieDuration;
        }
    }

    expires.setMinutes(expires.getMinutes() + cExpiry);

    // Sets cookie if we have to clear (block -> non-blocked state) OR
    // set with value (non-block -> block state)
    if ((thamba && daTrk === '0') || (!thamba && daTrk === '1')) {
        w.wafer.utils.setCookie(cookieName, daTrk, {expires: expires, domain: location.hostname, path:'/'});
    }

    // if (dabConfig.enableABPDetection && daTrk === '1') { // will uncomment when we can detect container collapsed
    if (dabConfig.enableABPDetection) {
        detectABP(daTrk);
    }
};

w.wafer && w.wafer.utils && w.wafer.ready  && w.wafer.ready(function () {
    setTimeout(initABDetection, dabConfig.detectionTimeout || 300);
});
